240 if (this.registered.length === this.scripts.length) {

241 this.registered.forEach(function (fn) {

242 if (typeof fn === 'function') {

243 setTimeout(fn, 0);

244 }

245 });

246 this.ready = function () {};

247 }

248 },

249

250 insert: function (s) {

251 var t = d.getElementById('js-position' + this.index);

252 if (t && t.insertAdjacentElement) {

253 t.insertAdjacentElement('afterend', s);

254 } else {

255 d.head.appendChild(s);

256 }

257 ++this.index;

258 },

259

260 createScript: function (script, beforeLoad) {

261 var s = d.createElement('script');

262 s.id = 'js-position' + (this.index + 1);

263 s.setAttribute('data-test', script.test);

264 if (beforeLoad) {

265 s.defer = 'defer';

266 s.onload = function () {

267 if (script.noinit) {

268 loader.register(true);

269 }

270 if (d.readyState === 'interactive' || d.readyState === 'complete') {

271 loader.ready();

272 }

273 };

274 } else {

275 s.async = 'async';

276 }

277 s.src = script.src;

278 return s;

279 },

280

281 init: function () {

282 this.scripts.forEach(function (s) {

283 loader.insert(loader.createScript(s, true));

284 });

285

286 d.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {

287 loader.ready();

288

289 var conditionalScripts = [

290 {match: 'div[data-pan-container]', src: '/static/js/pan-zoom-es6-bundle-464a2af269.js', test: 'pan-zoom-js', module: true },

291 {match: 'div[data-pan-container]', src: '/static/js/pan-zoom-es5-bundle-2626f1bdf8.js', test: 'pan-zoom-js', nomodule: true },

292 {match: 'math,span.mathjax-tex', src: '/static/js/math-es6-bundle-d616f8e4f9.js', test: 'math-js', module: true},

293 {match: 'math,span.mathjax-tex', src: '/static/js/math-es5-bundle-66109c5184.js', test: 'math-js', nomodule: true}

294 ];

295

296

297 if (conditionalScripts) {

298 conditionalScripts.filter(function (script) {

299 return !!document.querySelector(script.match) && !((moduleSupport && script.nomodule) || (!moduleSupport && script.module));

300 }).forEach(function (script) {

301 loader.insert(loader.createScript(script));

302 });

303 }

304 }, false);

305 }

306 };

307 loader.init();

308 }

309 })(window, document);

310</script>

356 <meta name="dc.description" content="In the bone marrow (BM) microenvironment, where breast cancer (BC)-disseminated tumor cells (DTCs) can remain dormant for decades, NG2+/Nestin+ mesenchymal stem cells (MSCs) promote hematopoietic stem cell quiescence. Here we reveal that periarteriolar BM-resident NG2+/Nestin+ MSCs can also instruct BC DTCs to enter dormancy. NG2+/Nestin+ MSCs produce transforming growth factor (TGF)-&#946;2 and bone morphogenetic protein (BMP)7 and activate a quiescence pathway dependent on TGFBRIII and BMPRII, which via p38-kinase, results in p27 induction. Genetic depletion of MSCs or conditional knockout of TGF-&#946;2 in MSCs using an NG2-CreER driver led to bone metastatic outgrowth of otherwise dormant p27+/Ki67&#8722; DTCs. Also, patients with estrogen receptor-positive BC without systemic recurrence displayed higher frequency of TGF-&#946;2 and BMP7 detection in the BM. Our results provide direct proof that hematopoietic stem cell dormancy niches control BC DTC dormancy and suggest that aging or extrinsic factors that affect the NG2+/Nestin+ MSC niche homeostasis may result in a break from dormancy and BC bone relapse. Aguirre-Ghiso and colleagues report that bone-marrow-resident mesenchymal stem cells promote cancer dormancy through TGF-&#946; family members."/>

889 <div class="c-article-body">

890 <section aria-labelledby="Abs1" data-title="Abstract" lang="en"><div class="c-article-section" id="Abs1-section"><h2 class="c-article-section__title js-section-title js-c-reading-companion-sections-item" id="Abs1">Abstract</h2><div class="c-article-section__content" id="Abs1-content"><p>In the bone marrow (BM) microenvironment, where breast cancer (BC)-disseminated tumor cells (DTCs) can remain dormant for decades, NG2<sup>+</sup>/Nestin<sup>+</sup> mesenchymal stem cells (MSCs) promote hematopoietic stem cell quiescence. Here we reveal that periarteriolar BM-resident NG2<sup>+</sup>/Nestin<sup>+</sup> MSCs can also instruct BC DTCs to enter dormancy. NG2<sup>+</sup>/Nestin<sup>+</sup> MSCs produce transforming growth factor (TGF)-β2 and bone morphogenetic protein (BMP)7 and activate a quiescence pathway dependent on TGFBRIII and BMPRII, which via p38-kinase, results in p27 induction. Genetic depletion of MSCs or conditional knockout of TGF-β2 in MSCs using an NG2-Cre<sup>ER</sup> driver led to bone metastatic outgrowth of otherwise dormant p27<sup>+</sup>/Ki67<sup>−</sup> DTCs. Also, patients with estrogen receptor-positive BC without systemic recurrence displayed higher frequency of TGF-β2 and BMP7 detection in the BM. Our results provide direct proof that hematopoietic stem cell dormancy niches control BC DTC dormancy and suggest that aging or extrinsic factors that affect the NG2<sup>+</sup>/Nestin<sup>+</sup> MSC niche homeostasis may result in a break from dormancy and BC bone relapse.</p></div></div></section>

1155 <section data-title="Data availability"><div class="c-article-section" id="data-availability-section"><h2 class="c-article-section__title js-section-title js-c-reading-companion-sections-item" id="data-availability">Data availability</h2><div class="c-article-section__content" id="data-availability-content">

1156

1157 <p>The data generated during the current study that support the reported findings are available in the manuscript, including in the provided Source Data files and from the corresponding author on reasonable request. <a data-track="click" data-track-label="link" data-track-action="section anchor" href="/articles/s43018-021-00179-8#Sec27">Source data</a> are provided with this paper.</p>

imaging-guided injection of cells into the left ventricle of the heart. This methodology ensures intracardiac injection efficiency, minimizing variability of injections on BM DTC burden analysis.</p></div></div></div></div></div></section><section data-title="Source
